FROM `Content` AS `c`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT FALSE AS `c`, `c0`.`Title`, `p`.`IdContent`, `p`.`IdParentContent`, `c0`.`Id`
    FROM `ParentContent` AS `p`
    INNER JOIN `Content` AS `c0` ON `p`.`IdContent` = `c0`.`Id`
) AS `t` ON `c`.`Id` = `t`.`IdParentContent`
